 court ne ko aadesh die the ki agar railway ne 35 lakh 44 hajaar rupee jamaa nahin kiye to guuruuvaar subah oona stesan par train jabt kar lee jaaegi
 Railways submitted two demand drafts of 26 lakh 53 thousand and 8 lakh 91 thousand to the court
 ye rakam do kisaan- melaram or madanlaal komuaavje ke taur par di jaaegi
 The bailiff of the court and the complainant were present at the station as per the order of High Voltage Dramacort run at Una railway station
 lekin railway vibhaag ke adhikariyon ne train chalane se mahaj das minute pehle demand draft kii copy adaalat ke karmchaaree ko saunpkar train ko jabt hone se bachaa liya

 railway ne oona se churudu section ke bich rail line bichaane ke liye kisaanon kii jameen lee thi

 lekin melaram or madanlaal kaa daawa tha ki unhen kam paise mili

 8 to Mailaram from the court
 91 lakh or madanlaal ko 26
 Instructions for giving additional compensation of Rs 53 lakh
 railway ne ise hoicourt main chunauti de di
 The High Court granted a stay but instructed the Railways to deposit the compensation amount in the court within three months
 railway ne phir bhi paise jamaa nahin karaae
 After this, the High Court dismissed the stay and told the farmers that they can appeal to the lower court for recovery of money
 loar court ne melaram or madanlaal ke paksh main faisla kiya

 ) paraprantiyon ke khilaaf shivasena ke agenda ko rahul gandhi ke aade haath lene kii koshishon kaa zikr karte hue nai dilli sthit america duutavas kii ore se beeti farvari main bheje gayi gopneey sandesh main kaha gaya ki yuva congress netaa siyasat main teji se pair jamaate najar aa rahe hai
 This 22 February 2010 confidential message has been revealed through wikileaks
 isamen 30 janvari se 19 farvari ke bich ke bharat ke raajnneetik ghatnakram kaa zikr he
 The document says that Gandhi's public relations strengthened after Gandhi's outburst against the 'raging nationalist party of Maharashtra' after the Mumbai tour
 mumbai daure ke dauraan unhone local train main bhi yatra kii
 The secret message said, 'rahul Gandhi's visit to Mumbai and his feud with the Shiv Sena, the militant nationalist party in Maharashtra, shows that he is fast gaining ground in politics
 ’ america ne vikiliks par gopneey sandesh churaane kaa aarope lagaaya he or in sandeshon kii pramanikta kii pushti karne yaa unka khandan karne se inkaar kar diya he
 The document said in reference to the political developments of the time, "he (gandhi) spoke a few words for the Shiv Sena's agenda against Thackeray and the Parupantis
 isaki desh bhar main vyapak or sahanubhutipurvak report hui
 "as per the confidential message," when Shiv Sena gave 'warnings to stay away from Maharashtra', he (rahul Gandhi) went a step further and went to the Thackeray family stronghold Mumbai and continued to take him there
 ’sandesh kahata he, ‘unhone (gandhi ne) kamaal to tab kar diya jab unhone apni yatra ke kaarykram main ain vakt par badlaav kar duusari shrenee ke dibbe main yatra kii or aam aadmi se judaav ko darshaya
